class RetryableUploadError(RuntimeError):
    """Upload failure that should be retried by queue scheduler."""


class NonRetryableUploadError(RuntimeError):
    """Upload failure that must not be retried by queue scheduler."""


class WorkerService:
    def __init__(self, config: Any, logger: Optional[logging.Logger] = None) -> None:
        self.config = config
        self.logger = logger or logging.getLogger("clonecut.worker.service")
        self.booted_at = time.time()
        self.redis_client = build_redis_client(
            host=str(getattr(config, "redis_host", "127.0.0.1")),
            port=int(getattr(config, "redis_port", 6379)),
            db=int(getattr(config, "redis_db", 0)),
            password=str(getattr(config, "redis_password", "")),
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        self.registry = RedisTaskRegistry(
            redis_client=self.redis_client,
            namespace=str(getattr(config, "redis_namespace", "clonecut_worker:")),
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        self.dedup_ttl_seconds = max(60, int(self._get_queue_cfg("dedup_ttl_seconds", 24 * 3600)))
        self.queue_adapter = RedisQueueAdapter(
            redis_client=self.redis_client,
            namespace=str(getattr(config, "redis_namespace", "clonecut_worker:")),
            dedup_ttl_seconds=self.dedup_ttl_seconds,
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        self.use_redis_queue = self.queue_adapter.is_persistent()

            "upload": 0,

            "running": 0,

        self.max_process_workers = max(1, int(self._get_worker_cfg("max_process_workers", 2)))

        self.active_task_ids: set[str] = set()

        self.upload_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        self.upload_storage_backend = str(

            api_endpoint=os.getenv("CLONECUT_TTS_API_ENDPOINT", tts_api_endpoint),

        video_timeout_raw = self._get_worker_cfg("video_command_timeout_seconds", 7200)

        self.video_adapter = ExternalVideoCommandAdapter(

                os.getenv("CLONECUT_VIDEO_COMMAND_TIMEOUT_SECONDS", str(video_timeout))
            ),
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        self.internal_pipeline_enabled = self._bool_cfg(
            os.getenv("CLONECUT_USE_INTERNAL_PIPELINE"),
            bool(self._get_worker_cfg("use_internal_pipeline", False)),
        )

        # --- telemetry ---
        telemetry_interval = float(self._get_worker_cfg("resource_monitor_interval_seconds", 5.0))
        report_dir = str(self._get_worker_cfg("performance_report_dir", "logs/performance_reports"))
        self.resource_monitor = ResourceMonitor(
            interval_seconds=telemetry_interval,
            disk_path=str(self.config.output_dir),
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        self.performance_tracker = PerformanceTracker(resource_monitor=self.resource_monitor)
        self.report_generator = ReportGenerator(report_dir=report_dir, logger=self.logger)

    def start(self) -> None:
        if any(thread.is_alive() for thread in self.worker_threads):
            return

        self.resource_monitor.start()
        recovered = self._recover_stuck_tasks()
        restored_retries = self._restore_retry_schedule()
        self.stop_event.clear()
        self.worker_threads = []
        self._spawn_workers("download", self.max_download_workers, self._download_loop)
        self._spawn_workers("process", self.max_process_workers, self._process_loop)
        self._spawn_workers("upload", self.max_upload_workers, self._upload_loop)
        self._spawn_workers("retry", 1, self._retry_scheduler_loop)
        self._spawn_workers("zombie", 1, self._zombie_cleaner_loop)

        self.logger.info(
            "worker adapters: tts_enabled=%s tts_engine=%s tts_http_ready=%s video_cmd_enabled=%s internal_pipeline=%s redis_registry=%s redis_queue=%s recovered=%s restored_retries=%s",
            self.tts_adapter_enabled,
            self.tts_engine_mode,
            self.tts_http_adapter.is_ready(),
            self.video_adapter.is_enabled(),
            self.internal_pipeline_enabled,
            self.registry.is_persistent(),
            self.use_redis_queue,
            recovered,
            restored_retries,
        )
        self.logger.info(
            "worker pools started: download=%s process=%s upload=%s retry_scheduler=%s zombie_timeout=%ss zombie_by_status=%s",
            self.max_download_workers,
            self.max_process_workers,
            self.max_upload_workers,
            1,
            self.zombie_timeout_seconds,
            self.zombie_timeout_by_status_seconds,
        )

    def stop(self) -> None:
        self.stop_event.set()
        for thread in self.worker_threads:
            thread.join(timeout=2.0)
        self.resource_monitor.stop()
        self.logger.info("worker service stopped")

    def submit(self, raw_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> Tuple[bool, str, Optional[str]]:
        try:
            task = self._build_task(raw_data)
        except ValueError as exc:
            return False, "", str(exc)

        existing_task_id = self.queue_adapter.check_duplicate(task)
        if existing_task_id:
            self.logger.info(
                "duplicate task ignored: incoming=%s existing=%s",
                task.task_id,
                existing_task_id,
            )
            return True, existing_task_id, None

        self._persist_task(task)
        self.queue_adapter.remember_dedup(task, ttl_seconds=self.dedup_ttl_seconds)
        self._enqueue_task(self._initial_queue_for_task(task), task)

        with self.lock:
            self.stats["received"] += 1

        self.logger.info(
            "task received: task_id=%s type=%s queued=%s",
            task.task_id,
            task.task_type.value,
            self._initial_queue_for_task(task),
        )
        return True, task.task_id, None

    def get_status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        queue_sizes = self.queue_adapter.get_queue_sizes()
        queued_total = (
            int(queue_sizes.get("download", 0))
            + int(queue_sizes.get("process", 0))
            + int(queue_sizes.get("upload", 0))
        )
        task_status_counts = self.get_task_status_counts()

        with self.lock:
            running = sum(self.active_workers.values())
            stats = dict(self.stats)
            active_workers = dict(self.active_workers)
        active_task_count = (
            int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.PENDING.value, 0))
            + int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.ASSIGNED.value, 0))
            + int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING.value, 0))
            + int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.PROCESSING.value, 0))
            + int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.UPLOADING.value, 0))
        )
        status_metrics = {
            "total": int(task_status_counts.get("total", 0)),
            "completed": int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.COMPLETED.value, 0)),
            "failed": int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.FAILED.value, 0)),
            "active": int(active_task_count),
            "zombie": int(stats["zombie_reclaimed"]),
            "retried": int(stats["retried"]),
            "received": int(stats["received"]),
        }

        return {
            "status": "online",
            "is_busy": running > 0 or queued_total > 0,
            "total_queue_size": queued_total + running,
            "queue_sizes": queue_sizes,
            "queues": {
                "download": int(queue_sizes.get("download", 0)),
                "process": int(queue_sizes.get("process", 0)),
                "upload": int(queue_sizes.get("upload", 0)),
                "pending": queued_total,
                "processing": active_workers.get("process", 0),
                "completed": stats["completed"],
                "failed": stats["failed"],
                "retried": stats["retried"],
                "received": stats["received"],
                "active": active_task_count,
                "total": int(task_status_counts.get("total", 0)),
                "zombie_reclaimed": stats["zombie_reclaimed"],
                "zombie": stats["zombie_reclaimed"],
            },
            "workers": active_workers,
            "status_metrics": status_metrics,
            "task_status_counts": task_status_counts,
            "uptime_seconds": int(max(0, time.time() - self.booted_at)),
            "timestamp": time.time(),
        }

    def get_resources(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return self.resource_monitor.get_current()

    def get_resources_history(self, minutes: int = 60) -> list:
        return self.resource_monitor.get_history(minutes=minutes)

    def get_task(self, task_id: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
        task = self.registry.get(task_id)
        if task is None:
            return None
        return task.to_dict()

    def get_task_status_counts(self) -> Dict[str, int]:
        counts: Dict[str, int] = {}
        for status in self._queryable_statuses():
            counts[status.value] = int(self.registry.count_by_status(status))
        counts["total"] = sum(counts.values())
        return counts

    def list_tasks(
        self,
        status: Optional[str] = None,
        limit: int = 20,
        offset: int = 0,
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        size = max(1, min(200, int(limit)))
        start = max(0, int(offset))
        target_statuses = self._resolve_status_filter(status)
        read_limit = min(5000, start + size)

        if len(target_statuses) == 1:
            selected = target_statuses[0]
            total = int(self.registry.count_by_status(selected))
            tasks = self.registry.list_by_status(selected, limit=max(1, read_limit))
        else:
            total = 0
            merged: Dict[str, UnifiedTask] = {}
            for st in target_statuses:
                total += int(self.registry.count_by_status(st))
                for task in self.registry.list_by_status(st, limit=max(1, read_limit)):
                    merged[task.task_id] = task
            tasks = list(merged.values())
            tasks.sort(key=lambda item: item.created_at, reverse=True)

        selected_tasks = tasks[start : start + size]
        return {
            "total": total,
            "limit": size,
            "offset": start,
            "tasks": [item.to_dict() for item in selected_tasks],
        }

    def cancel_task(self, task_id: str) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        task = self.registry.get(task_id)
        if task is None:
            return False, "task not found"
        if task.status == TaskStatus.CANCELLED:
            return True, ""
        if task.status == TaskStatus.COMPLETED:
            return False, "completed task cannot be cancelled"
        if task.status in {TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING, TaskStatus.PROCESSING, TaskStatus.UPLOADING}:
            return False, f"task is running in status={task.status.value}, cannot be cancelled safely"

        transitioned = self._transition_status(task, TaskStatus.CANCELLED, strict=False)
        if not transitioned:
            return False, f"illegal transition: {task.status.value} -> cancelled"
        task.stage_checkpoint = "cancelled"
        task.error_message = None
        task.metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
        task.metadata["cancelled_at"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
        self._persist_task(task)
        return True, ""

    def retry_task(self, task_id: str) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        task = self.registry.get(task_id)
        if task is None:
            return False, "task not found"
        if task.status != TaskStatus.FAILED:
            return False, f"only failed task can retry, current={task.status.value}"

        self._remove_retry_schedule(task.task_id)
        if int(task.retry_count) >= int(task.max_retries):
            task.max_retries = int(task.retry_count) + 1

        task.metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
        task.metadata["manual_retry"] = True
        task.metadata["manual_retry_at"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
        self._enqueue_retry_task(task)
        with self.lock:
            self.stats["retried"] += 1
        return True, ""

    def _download_loop(self) -> None:
        while not self.stop_event.is_set():
            task = self._dequeue_stage_task("download")
            if task is None:
                continue
            self._mark_stage_active("download", +1)
            self._mark_task_active(task.task_id, True)
            try:
                self._ru…13332 tokens truncated…      payload.get("hotwords"),
            metadata.get("hotwords"),
            merged.get("keywords"),
            payload.get("keywords"),
            metadata.get("keywords"),
        )
        if hotwords:
            merged["hotwords"] = hotwords

        cover_up = self._pick_first_text(
            merged.get("cover_title_up"),
            merged.get("封面标题上"),
            payload.get("cover_title_up"),
            payload.get("封面标题上"),
            metadata.get("cover_title_up"),
            metadata.get("封面标题上"),
        )
        cover_middle = self._pick_first_text(
            merged.get("cover_title_middle"),
            merged.get("封面标题中"),
            payload.get("cover_title_middle"),
            payload.get("封面标题中"),
            metadata.get("cover_title_middle"),
            metadata.get("封面标题中"),
        )
        cover_down = self._pick_first_text(
            merged.get("cover_title_down"),
            merged.get("封面标题下"),
            payload.get("cover_title_down"),
            payload.get("封面标题下"),
            metadata.get("cover_title_down"),
            metadata.get("封面标题下"),
        )

        cover_titles = self._normalize_text_list(merged.get("cover_titles"))
        if not cover_up and len(cover_titles) >= 1:
            cover_up = cover_titles[0]
        if not cover_middle and len(cover_titles) >= 2:
            cover_middle = cover_titles[1]
        if not cover_down and len(cover_titles) >= 3:
            cover_down = cover_titles[2]

        compact_titles = [text for text in (cover_up, cover_middle, cover_down) if text]
        if compact_titles:
            merged["cover_titles"] = compact_titles
            merged["cover_title_up"] = cover_up
            merged["cover_title_middle"] = cover_middle
            merged["cover_title_down"] = cover_down
            merged["封面标题上"] = cover_up
            merged["封面标题中"] = cover_middle
            merged["封面标题下"] = cover_down

        speaker = self._pick_first_text(
            merged.get("speaker"),
            merged.get("speaker_id"),
            merged.get("spk"),
            merged.get("target_speaker"),
        )
        if speaker:
            merged["speaker"] = speaker

        original_filename = self._resolve_original_filename(
            forum_post_info=merged,
            payload=payload,
            metadata=metadata,
            source_url="",
        )
        if original_filename:
            merged["original_filename"] = original_filename
        return merged

    def _normalize_text_list(self, *values: Any) -> List[str]:
        output: List[str] = []
        seen: set[str] = set()
        for value in values:
            items: List[str] = []
            if isinstance(value, list):
                items = [str(item or "").strip() for item in value]
            elif isinstance(value, str):
                items = [item.strip() for item in value.replace("\uFF0C", ",").split(",")]
            for item in items:
                normalized = " ".join(item.split())
                if not normalized:
                    continue
                dedup_key = normalized.lower()
                if dedup_key in seen:
                    continue
                seen.add(dedup_key)
                output.append(normalized)
        return output

    def _pick_first_text(self, *values: Any) -> str:
        for value in values:
            text = str(value or "").strip()
            if text:
                return text
        return ""

    def _sanitize_filename(self, value: str) -> str:
        text = str(value or "").strip()
        if not text:
            return ""
        text = text.replace("\\", "/").split("/")[-1].strip()
        text = re.sub(r"[\x00-\x1f]", "", text)
        text = re.sub(r"[<>:\"/\\\\|?*]+", "_", text)
        text = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", text).strip().strip(".")
        return text

    def _init_task_storage(self) -> Optional[SqliteStorageAdapter]:
        db_path = os.getenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", "data/clonecut.db")
        try:
            return SqliteStorageAdapter(db_path=db_path, logger=self.logger)
        except Exception as exc:
            self.logger.warning("sqlite storage disabled: %s", exc)
            return None

    def _save_task_snapshot(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> None:
        self._sync_task_metadata(task)
        if self.task_storage is None:
            return
        self.task_storage.save_task(task)

    def _persist_task(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> None:
        self._sync_task_metadata(task)
        self.registry.add(task)
        self._save_task_snapshot(task)

    def _sync_task_metadata(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> None:
        metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
        metadata["current_stage"] = int(task.current_stage)
        metadata["max_retries"] = int(task.max_retries)
        metadata["retry_count"] = int(task.retry_count)
        if task.stage_checkpoint:
            metadata["stage_checkpoint"] = task.stage_checkpoint
        else:
            metadata.pop("stage_checkpoint", None)
        task.metadata = metadata

    def _transition_status(self, task: UnifiedTask, status: TaskStatus, strict: bool = True) -> bool:
        result = self.registry.update_status(task.task_id, status)
        if result.ok:
            task.status = status
            if status in {TaskStatus.PENDING, TaskStatus.FAILED, TaskStatus.CANCELLED}:
                task.started_at = None
            return True
        if strict:
            raise RuntimeError(result.reason or f"status transition failed: {task.task_id}")
        return False

    def _mark_task_active(self, task_id: str, active: bool) -> None:
        with self.lock:
            if active:
                self.active_task_ids.add(task_id)
            else:
                self.active_task_ids.discard(task_id)

    def _schedule_retry(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> bool:
        if task.status != TaskStatus.FAILED:
            return False
        retryable = bool((task.metadata or {}).get("retryable_failure", True))
        if not retryable:
            return False
        max_retries = max(0, int(task.max_retries))
        if task.retry_count >= max_retries:
            return False

        delay = self._retry_delay_seconds(task, task.retry_count)
        retry_count = task.retry_count + 1
        due_at = time.time() + delay
        task.retry_count = retry_count
        task.metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
        task.metadata["retry_due_at"] = due_at
        task.metadata["retry_delay_seconds"] = delay
        self._persist_task(task)

        with self.lock:
            self.retry_index[task.task_id] = (due_at, task)
            heapq.heappush(self.retry_heap, (due_at, task.task_id))
            self.stats["retried"] += 1
        return True

    def _retry_delay_seconds(self, task: UnifiedTask, retry_count_before_increment: int) -> int:
        failed_from = str((task.metadata or {}).get("failed_from_status", "")).strip().lower()
        backoff = self.retry_backoff_seconds or [5]
        if failed_from == TaskStatus.UPLOADING.value:
            backoff = self.upload_retry_backoff_seconds or [1, 2, 4]
        idx = min(max(0, int(retry_count_before_increment)), len(backoff) - 1)
        return int(backoff[idx])

    def _is_retryable_failure(self, error: Exception, failed_from: TaskStatus) -> bool:
        if failed_from != TaskStatus.UPLOADING:
            return True
        if isinstance(error, RetryableUploadError):
            return True
        if isinstance(error, NonRetryableUploadError):
            return False
        return False

    def _remove_retry_schedule(self, task_id: str) -> None:
        with self.lock:
            self.retry_index.pop(task_id, None)

    def _retry_scheduler_loop(self) -> None:
        while not self.stop_event.is_set():
            ready = self._dequeue_ready_retries()
            for task in ready:
                self._enqueue_retry_task(task)
            self.stop_event.wait(self.retry_check_interval_seconds)

    def _dequeue_ready_retries(self) -> List[UnifiedTask]:
        now_ts = time.time()
        ready: List[UnifiedTask] = []
        with self.lock:
            while self.retry_heap:
                due_at, task_id = self.retry_heap[0]
                if due_at > now_ts:
                    break
                heapq.heappop(self.retry_heap)
                indexed = self.retry_index.get(task_id)
                if indexed is None:
                    continue
                idx_due_at, task = indexed
                if idx_due_at != due_at:
                    continue
                self.retry_index.pop(task_id, None)
                ready.append(task)
        return ready

    def _enqueue_retry_task(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> None:
        queue_name = self._queue_for_retry_task(task)
        task.metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
        task.metadata.pop("retry_due_at", None)
        task.metadata.pop("retry_delay_seconds", None)
        task.metadata.pop("retryable_failure", None)
        task.error_message = None
        task.completed_at = None
        task.started_at = None
        transitioned = self._transition_status(task, TaskStatus.PENDING, strict=False)
        if not transitioned:
            task.status = TaskStatus.PENDING
            self._persist_task(task)
        else:
            self._persist_task(task)
        if queue_name == "upload":
            transitioned_upload = self._transition_status(task, TaskStatus.PROCESSING, strict=False)
            if not transitioned_upload:
                task.status = TaskStatus.PROCESSING
            self._persist_task(task)
        self._enqueue_task(queue_name, task)
        self.logger.info(
            "task retry enqueued: task_id=%s retry_count=%s/%s queue=%s",
            task.task_id,
            task.retry_count,
            task.max_retries,
            queue_name,
        )

    def _queue_for_retry_task(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> str:
        failed_from = str((task.metadata or {}).get("failed_from_status", "")).strip().lower()
        if failed_from == TaskStatus.UPLOADING.value and self._has_uploadable_output(task):
            return "upload"
        if failed_from == TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING.value and self._needs_download(task):
            return "download"
        if failed_from == TaskStatus.PROCESSING.value:
            return "process"
        return self._initial_queue_for_task(task)

    def _restore_retry_schedule(self) -> int:
        if not self.registry.is_persistent():
            return 0
        tasks = self.registry.list_by_status(TaskStatus.FAILED, limit=5000)
        restored = 0
        now_ts = time.time()
        for task in tasks:
            if int(task.retry_count) >= int(task.max_retries):
                continue
            retry_due_at_raw = (task.metadata or {}).get("retry_due_at")
            try:
                retry_due_at = float(retry_due_at_raw)
            except Exception:
                retry_due_at = now_ts
            with self.lock:
                self.retry_index[task.task_id] = (retry_due_at, task)
                heapq.heappush(self.retry_heap, (retry_due_at, task.task_id))
            restored += 1
        return restored

    def _zombie_cleaner_loop(self) -> None:
        while not self.stop_event.is_set():
            reclaimed = self._reclaim_zombies_once()
            if reclaimed > 0:
                with self.lock:
                    self.stats["zombie_reclaimed"] += reclaimed
            self.stop_event.wait(self.zombie_check_interval_seconds)

    def _reclaim_zombies_once(self) -> int:
        running_statuses = [
            TaskStatus.PENDING,
            TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING,
            TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
            TaskStatus.UPLOADING,
        ]
        reclaimed = 0
        for status in running_statuses:
            tasks = self.registry.list_by_status(status, limit=2000)
            for task in tasks:
                if status != TaskStatus.PENDING:
                    with self.lock:
                        if task.task_id in self.active_task_ids:
                            continue
                if not self._is_zombie_task(task, status):
                    continue
                age = int((datetime.now() - (task.started_at or task.created_at)).total_seconds())
                error = RuntimeError(
                    f"zombie task reclaimed after {age}s in status={status.value}"
                )
                self._fail_task(task, error, failed_from=status)
                reclaimed += 1
        return reclaimed

    def _is_zombie_task(self, task: UnifiedTask, status: TaskStatus) -> bool:
        timeout_seconds = float(
            self.zombie_timeout_by_status_seconds.get(status.value, self.zombie_timeout_seconds)
        )
        if timeout_seconds <= 0:
            return False
        if status == TaskStatus.PENDING:
            started_at = task.created_at
        else:
            started_at = task.started_at or task.assigned_at or task.created_at
        if started_at is None:
            return False
        age = (datetime.now() - started_at).total_seconds()
        return age > timeout_seconds

    def _build_zombie_timeout_by_status(self) -> Dict[str, float]:
        mapping_raw = self._get_worker_cfg("zombie_timeout_by_status_seconds", {})
        mapping = mapping_raw if isinstance(mapping_raw, dict) else {}
        defaults = {
            TaskStatus.PENDING.value: float(self.zombie_timeout_seconds),
            TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING.value: float(self.zombie_timeout_seconds),
            TaskStatus.PROCESSING.value: float(self.zombie_timeout_seconds),
            TaskStatus.UPLOADING.value: float(self.zombie_timeout_seconds),
        }
        resolved: Dict[str, float] = {}
        for status_value, default in defaults.items():
            per_status_key = f"zombie_timeout_{status_value}_seconds"
            per_status_value = self._get_worker_cfg(per_status_key, None)
            if per_status_value is not None:
                resolved[status_value] = self._coerce_timeout_seconds(per_status_value, default)
                continue
            map_value = mapping.get(status_value)
            if map_value is not None:
                resolved[status_value] = self._coerce_timeout_seconds(map_value, default)
                continue
            resolved[status_value] = float(default)
        return resolved

    def _coerce_timeout_seconds(self, value: Any, default: float) -> float:
        try:
            return max(5.0, float(value))
        except Exception:
            return max(5.0, float(default))

    def _recover_stuck_tasks(self) -> int:
        if not self.registry.is_persistent():
            return 0

        recoverable = [
            TaskStatus.ASSIGNED,
            TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING,
            TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
            TaskStatus.UPLOADING,
        ]
        recovered = 0
        for status in recoverable:
            tasks = self.registry.list_by_status(status, limit=2000)
            for task in tasks:
                queue_name = self._recovery_queue_for_task(task, status)
                next_status = TaskStatus.PROCESSING if queue_name == "upload" else TaskStatus.PENDING
                task.status = next_status
                if next_status == TaskStatus.PENDING:
                    task.started_at = None
                else:
                    task.started_at = task.started_at or datetime.now()
                task.completed_at = None
                self._persist_task(task)
                self._enqueue_task(queue_name, task)
                recovered += 1
        return recovered

    def _recovery_queue_for_task(self, task: UnifiedTask, old_status: TaskStatus) -> str:
        if old_status == TaskStatus.UPLOADING and self._has_uploadable_output(task):
            return "upload"
        if old_status == TaskStatus.PROCESSING:
            return "process"
        if old_status == TaskStatus.FAILED:
            return self._queue_for_retry_task(task)
        if old_status == TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING and self._needs_download(task):
            return "download"
        return self._initial_queue_for_task(task)

    def _get_queue_cfg(self, key: str, default: Any) -> Any:
        raw_queue = {}
        if isinstance(getattr(self.config, "raw", None), dict):
            raw_queue = self.config.raw.get("queue", {}) or {}
        env_key = f"CLONECUT_QUEUE_{key}".upper()
        env_val = os.getenv(env_key)
        if env_val is not None:
            return self._cast_cfg_value(env_val, default)
        if key in raw_queue:
            return self._cast_cfg_value(raw_queue.get(key), default)
        return default

    def _parse_retry_backoff(self, raw: Any) -> List[int]:
        if isinstance(raw, list):
            values = raw
        elif isinstance(raw, str):
            text = raw.strip()
            values = [item.strip() for item in text.split(",") if item.strip()]
        else:
            values = [5, 10, 20]

        parsed: List[int] = []
        for item in values:
            try:
                parsed.append(max(1, int(item)))
            except Exception:
                continue
        if not parsed:
            parsed = [5, 10, 20]
        return parsed

    def _get_worker_cfg(self, key: str, default: Any) -> Any:
        raw_worker = {}
        if isinstance(getattr(self.config, "raw", None), dict):
            raw_worker = self.config.raw.get("worker", {}) or {}

        env_key = f"CLONECUT_WORKER_{key}".upper()
        env_val = os.getenv(env_key)
        if env_val is not None:
            return self._cast_cfg_value(env_val, default)
        if key in raw_worker:
            return self._cast_cfg_value(raw_worker.get(key), default)
        return default

    def _cast_cfg_value(self, value: Any, default: Any) -> Any:
        if isinstance(default, bool):
            if isinstance(value, bool):
                return value
            return str(value).strip().lower() == "true"
        if isinstance(default, int):
            try:
                return int(value)
            except Exception:
                return default
        if isinstance(default, float):
            try:
                return float(value)
            except Exception:
                return default
        return value

    def _bool_cfg(self, raw: Optional[str], default: bool) -> bool:
        if raw is None:
            return default
        return raw.strip().lower() == "true"

    def _queryable_statuses(self) -> List[TaskStatus]:
        return [
            TaskStatus.PENDING,
            TaskStatus.ASSIGNED,
            TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING,
            TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
            TaskStatus.UPLOADING,
            TaskStatus.COMPLETED,
            TaskStatus.FAILED,
            TaskStatus.CANCELLED,
        ]

    def _resolve_status_filter(self, status: Optional[str]) -> List[TaskStatus]:
        if status is None:
            return self._queryable_statuses()
        raw = str(status).strip().lower()
        if not raw or raw == "all":
            return self._queryable_statuses()
        known = {item.value for item in self._queryable_statuses()}
        if raw not in known:
            raise ValueError(f"invalid status filter: {status}")
        return [parse_task_status(raw)]


__all__ = ["WorkerService"]

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- encoding: utf-8 -*-

包含视频处理流水线所需的通用工具函数

# 设置日志记录
def setup_logging():
    """设置日志记录配置"""
    # 确保logs目录存在
    os.makedirs("logs", exist_ok=True)
    
    # 获取根日志记录器
    root_logger = logging.getLogger()
    
    # 清除所有现有处理器，避免重复输出
    if root_logger.handlers:
        root_logger.handlers.clear()
    
    # 创建处理器
    file_handler = logging.FileHandler(
        "logs/video_pipeline.log", 
        encoding='utf-8',
        errors='replace'
    )
    console_handler = logging.StreamHandler()
    
    # 创建格式化器
    formatter = logging.Formatter('%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
    file_handler.setFormatter(formatter)
    console_handler.setFormatter(formatter)
    
    # 配置根日志记录器
    root_logger.setLevel(logging.INFO)
    root_logger.addHandler(file_handler)
    root_logger.addHandler(console_handler)
    
    return logging

# 初始化日志
logging = setup_logging()

# 带超时的输入函数
def input_with_timeout(prompt, timeout=None, default="", skip_timeout=False):
    """带超时的输入函数
    
    参数:
        prompt: 提示信息
        timeout: 超时时间（秒），如果为None则从配置读取
        default: 超时后返回的默认值
        skip_timeout: 是否跳过超时等待直接返回默认值
        
    返回:
        用户输入或超时后的默认值
    """
    # 如果未指定超时时间，从配置读取
    if timeout is None:
        try:
            from pre.stage.config import get_config
            config = get_config()
            timeout = config.get("input_wait_time", 5)
        except:
            # 如果无法获取配置，使用默认值5秒
            timeout = 5
            
    # 如果跳过超时等待，直接返回默认值
    if skip_timeout:
        print(f"{prompt}")
        return default
        
    # 显示带有倒计时提示的提示信息
    print(f"{prompt}（{timeout}秒内无输入将使用默认选项: {default}）")
    
    # 在Windows上使用线程实现
    if platform.system() == 'Windows':
        import threading
        import queue
        
        # 使用队列存储用户输入
        user_input = queue.Queue()
        
        # 输入线程函数
        def input_thread():
            try:
                user_input.put(input())
            except:
                user_input.put(None)
        
        # 启动输入线程
        thread = threading.Thread(target=input_thread)
        thread.daemon = True
        thread.start()
        
        # 等待输入或超时
        try:
            result = user_input.get(timeout=timeout)
            if result is None:
                return default
            return result
        except queue.Empty:
            # 超时，使用默认值
            print(f"\n超时，使用默认选项: {default}")
            return default
    # Linux/Unix系统使用select模块
    else:
        rlist, _, _ = select.select([sys.stdin], [], [], timeout)
        if rlist:
            return input().strip()
        else:
            print(f"\n超时，使用默认选项: {default}")
            return default

def handle_ffmpeg_process(process):
    """
    处理FFmpeg进程的输出，实时显示进度信息
    
    Args:
        process: 通过subprocess.Popen创建的FFmpeg进程对象
        
    Returns:
        退出码, stdout内容, stderr内容
    """
    stdout_lines = []
    stderr_lines = []
    
    # 创建处理专用的子记录器
    ffmpeg_logger = logging.getLogger("ffmpeg_process")
    
    # 跟踪是否打印了进度信息，避免进度信息后多余的换行
    has_progress_output = False
    last_progress_line = ""
    
    # 记录开始时间，用于计算处理时长
    start_time = time.time()
    ffmpeg_logger.debug(f"FFmpeg进程启动，PID: {process.pid}")
    
    try:
        # 读取标准输出
        for line in iter(process.stdout.readline, ""):
            if not line:
                break
            
            # 确保处理字符串，不处理bytes
            if isinstance(line, bytes):
                try:
                    line = line.decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
                except Exception as e:
                    line = str(line) + f" [解码错误: {str(e)}]"
                    
            cleaned_line = line.strip()
            stdout_lines.append(cleaned_line)
            
            # 检查是否为进度信息（通常包含时间、比特率等）
            is_progress = any(keyword in line for keyword in ['time=', 'size=', 'bitrate=', 'speed='])
            if is_progress:
                # 只有当进度信息与上一行不同时才打印，避免刷屏
                if cleaned_line != last_progress_line:
                    print(cleaned_line, end='\r')
                    # 记录进度，但设置为DEBUG级别，避免日志文件过大
                    ffmpeg_logger.debug(f"进度: {cleaned_line}")
                    last_progress_line = cleaned_line
                    has_progress_output = True
            else:
                # 如果之前有进度信息，先打印一个换行，然后再打印非进度信息
                if has_progress_output:
                    print()
                    has_progress_output = False
                print(cleaned_line)
                # 记录非进度信息
                ffmpeg_logger.debug(f"标准输出: {cleaned_line}")
        
        # 读取标准错误
        for line in iter(process.stderr.readline, ""):
            if not line:
                break
                
            # 确保处理字符串，不处理bytes
            if isinstance(line, bytes):
                try:
                    line = line.decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
                except Exception as e:
                    line = str(line) + f" [解码错误: {str(e)}]"
            
            cleaned_line = line.strip()
            stderr_lines.append(cleaned_line)
            
            # 检查是否包含关键错误信息
            is_error = any(keyword in line.lower() for keyword in ['error', 'cannot', 'failed', 'not found', 'no such', 'invalid'])
            
            # 检查是否包含常见的路径错误信息
            is_path_error = any(keyword in line.lower() for keyword in ['no such file', 'cannot open', 'invalid argument', 'does not exist', 'directory not found'])
            
            # 如果是路径错误，记录更详细的信息用于调试
            if is_path_error:
                ffmpeg_logger.error(f"检测到路径错误: {cleaned_line}")
                print(f"FFmpeg路径错误: {cleaned_line}")
                # 如果之前有进度信息，确保打印换行
                if has_progress_output:
                    print()
                    has_progress_output = False
            # 如果是一般错误，也进行记录
            elif is_error:
                ffmpeg_logger.error(f"FFmpeg错误: {cleaned_line}")
                # 如果之前有进度信息，确保打印换行
                if has_progress_output:
                    print()
                    has_progress_output = False
                print(f"FFmpeg错误: {cleaned_line}")
            # 其他错误输出作为警告处理
            else:
                ffmpeg_logger.warning(f"FFmpeg信息: {cleaned_line}")
        
        # 等待进程完成
        process.wait()
        return_code = process.returncode
        
        # 检查返回码
        if return_code != 0:
            ffmpeg_logger.error(f"FFmpeg进程异常退出，返回码: {return_code}")
            if stderr_lines:
                ffmpeg_logger.error(f"FFmpeg错误详情: {stderr_lines[-1] if stderr_lines else 'No error details'}")
        else:
            # 计算处理时长
            elapsed = time.time() - start_time
            ffmpeg_logger.debug(f"FFmpeg进程正常完成，耗时: {elapsed:.2f}秒")
            
        # 如果显示了进度，在最后添加换行
        if has_progress_output:
            print()
            
        # 返回处理结果
        return return_code, '\n'.join(stdout_lines), '\n'.join(stderr_lines)
    
    except Exception as e:
        ffmpeg_logger.error(f"处理FFmpeg进程时出错: {str(e)}", exc_info=True)
        # 尝试终止进程
        try:
            process.kill()
        except:
            pass
        
        # 如果显示了进度，在最后添加换行
        if has_progress_output:
            print()
            
        return 1, '\n'.join(stdout_lines), f"处理FFmpeg进程时发生内部错误: {str(e)}\n" + '\n'.join(stderr_lines)

def run_command(cmd, step_name="", show_output=True, config=None):
    """
    运行命令并处理输出
    
    参数:
        cmd: 要执行的命令（列表或字符串）
        step_name: 步骤名称，用于日志记录
        show_output: 是否显示输出
        config: 配置参数字典
        
    返回:
        (成功标志, 输出消息, stdout内容)
    """
    if isinstance(cmd, list):
        cmd_str = " ".join(cmd)
    else:
        cmd_str = cmd
        cmd = cmd.split()
    
    if config and config.get("show_command", True):
        logging.info(f"执行命令: {cmd_str}")
    elif config is None:
        logging.info(f"执行命令: {cmd_str}")
    
    try:
        start_time = datetime.datetime.now()
        
        # 执行命令并捕获输出
        process = subprocess.Popen(
            cmd,
            stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
            stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
            universal_newlines=True
        )
        
        # 实时显示输出
        stdout_lines = []
        stderr_lines = []
        
        # 读取并处理标准输出
        has_progress_output = False
        last_progress_line = ""  # 存储最后一行进度信息，避免重复显示同类信息
        
        for line in iter(process.stdout.readline, ""):
            if not line:
                break
            stdout_lines.append(line.strip())
            if show_output:
                # 检查是否为进度信息（通常包含百分比或进度条）
                is_progress = any(keyword in line for keyword in ['%', 'progress', '进度', '[='])
                if is_progress:
                    # 只有当进度信息与上一行不同时才打印，避免刷屏
                    if line.strip() != last_progress_line:
                        print(line.strip(), end='\r')
                        last_progress_line = line.strip()
                        has_progress_output = True
                else:
                    # 如果之前有进度信息，先打印一个换行，然后再打印非进度信息
                    if has_progress_output:
                        print()
                        has_progress_output = False
                    print(line.strip())
        
        # 读取并处理标准错误
        last_progress_line = ""  # 重置进度信息跟踪
        for line in iter(process.stderr.readline, ""):
            if not line:
                break
            stderr_lines.append(line.strip())
            if show_output:
                # 检查是否为进度信息（通常包含百分比或进度条）
                is_progress = any(keyword in line for keyword in ['%', 'progress', '进度', 'time=', '[='])
                if is_progress:
                    # 只有当进度信息与上一行不同时才打印，避免刷屏
                    if line.strip() != last_progress_line:
                        print(line.strip(), end='\r', file=sys.stderr)
                        last_progress_line = line.strip()
                        has_progress_output = True
                else:
                    # 如果之前有进度信息，先打印一个换行，然后再打印非进度信息
                    if has_progress_output:
                        print()
                        has_progress_output = False
                    print(line.strip(), file=sys.stderr)
        
        # 如果有进度输出，打印换行确保后续内容从新行开始
        if has_progress_output:
            print()
        
        # 等待进程完成
        return_code = process.wait()
        end_time = datetime.datetime.now()
        elapsed = (end_time - start_time).total_seconds()
        
        if return_code == 0:
            logging.info(f"{step_name}成功完成，用时: {elapsed:.2f}秒")
            return True, "成功", "\n".join(stdout_lines)
        else:
            error_msg = "\n".join(stderr_lines) if stderr_lines else "未知错误"
            logging.error(f"{step_name}失败，退出码: {return_code}\n错误: {error_msg}")
            return False, error_msg, "\n".join(stdout_lines)
            
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"{step_name}执行出错: {str(e)}")
        return False, str(e), ""

def ensure_output_dir(output_dir):
    """确保输出目录存在"""
    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)

def get_output_video_path(output, input_video, output_dir):
    """从输出中提取生成的视频路径或基于输入视频生成预期路径"""
    # 尝试从输出中提取路径
    match = re.search(r"处理后的视频已保存至:\s*(.+\.mp4)", output)
    if match:
        return match.group(1)
    
    # 如果没找到，根据命名规则生成路径
    base_name = os.path.basename(input_video)
    name_without_ext, _ = os.path.splitext(base_name)
    
    # 检查转码或去静音路径
    trans_path = os.path.join(output_dir, f"{name_without_ext}_转码版.mp4")
    if os.path.exists(trans_path):
        return trans_path
    
    # 原来的_fast.mp4路径作为备选
    old_trans_path = os.path.join(output_dir, f"{name_without_ext}_fast.mp4")
    if os.path.exists(old_trans_path):
        return old_trans_path
    
    nosilence_path = os.path.join(output_dir, f"{name_without_ext}_去气口版.mp4")
    if os.path.exists(nosilence_path):
        return nosilence_path
    
    # 原来的_nosilence.mp4路径作为备选
    old_nosilence_path = os.path.join(output_dir, f"{name_without_ext}_nosilence.mp4")
    if os.path.exists(old_nosilence_path):
        return old_nosilence_path
    
    # 返回原路径
    return input_video

def format_srt_time(seconds):
    """将秒数格式化为SRT时间格式 HH:MM:SS,mmm"""
    hours = int(seconds / 3600)
    minutes = int((seconds % 3600) / 60)
    seconds = seconds % 60
    milliseconds = int((seconds - int(seconds)) * 1000)
    return f"{hours:02d}:{minutes:02d}:{int(seconds):02d},{milliseconds:03d}"

def save_state(step, input_file, output_file, output_dir):
    """保存当前处理步骤的状态"""
    # 规范化路径，确保在所有操作系统上使用正确的路径分隔符
    input_abs_path = os.path.normpath(os.path.abspath(input_file)) if input_file else None
    output_abs_path = os.path.normpath(os.path.abspath(output_file)) if output_file else None
    
    # 不再计算相对路径，避免跨驱动器问题
    # 保存状态信息，只存储绝对路径
    state = {
        "last_completed_step": step,
        "input_file": input_abs_path,  # 使用绝对路径
        "output_file": output_abs_path,  # 使用绝对路径
        "timestamp": datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    }
    
    # 保存到state文件
    state_path = os.path.join(output_dir, "pipeline_state.json")
    with open(state_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        json.dump(state, f, indent=4, ensure_ascii=False)
    
    print(f"已保存状态: 完成步骤 {step}, 输出文件: {output_file}")
    logging.info(f"已保存状态: 完成步骤 {step}, 绝对路径: {output_abs_path}")

def load_state(output_dir):
    """加载上一次保存的状态"""
    state_file = os.path.join(output_dir, "pipeline_state.json")
    if os.path.exists(state_file):
        try:
            with open(state_file, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                state = json.load(f)
            
            # 检查并尝试不同的路径方式
            output_file = None
            output_rel_path = state.get('output_file')
            output_abs_path = state.get('output_file_abs')
            
            # 先尝试相对路径
            if output_rel_path and os.path.exists(output_rel_path):
                output_file = output_rel_path
                logging.info(f"成功使用相对路径找到文件: {output_file}")
            # 再尝试绝对路径
            elif output_abs_path and os.path.exists(output_abs_path):
                output_file = output_abs_path
                logging.info(f"成功使用绝对路径找到文件: {output_file}")
            # 尝试其他可能的路径格式
            elif output_rel_path:
                alt_path = output_rel_path.replace('\\', '/')
                if os.path.exists(alt_path):
                    output_file = alt_path
                    logging.info(f"成功使用替代路径格式找到文件: {output_file}")
            
            # 更新状态中的输出文件为找到的有效路径
            if output_file:
                state['output_file'] = output_file
                print(f"加载上一次状态: 完成步骤 {state['last_completed_step']}, 输出文件: {output_file}")
                print(f"处理时间: {state['timestamp']}")
                return state
            else:
                logging.warning(f"无法找到状态文件中指定的输出文件: {output_rel_path} 或 {output_abs_path}")
                print(f"警告: 找不到上次处理的文件，将尝试查找最新视频")
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"读取状态文件失败: {e}")
            print(f"读取状态文件失败: {e}")
    return None

def find_latest_processed_video(output_dir):
    """查找output目录中最新处理的视频文件"""
    try:
        # 查找可能的处理后视频文件
        # 首先尝试查找 _去气口版.mp4 结尾的文件（第二步输出）
        nosilence_files = glob.glob(os.path.join(output_dir, "*_去气口版.mp4"))
        # 兼容老文件命名
        old_nosilence_files = glob.glob(os.path.join(output_dir, "*_nosilence.mp4"))
        nosilence_files.extend(old_nosilence_files)
        
        if nosilence_files:
            # 按修改时间排序，返回最新的
            return sorted(nosilence_files, key=os.path.getmtime, reverse=True)[0]
            
        # 如果没有找到，尝试查找 _转码版.mp4 结尾的文件（第一步输出）
        fast_files = glob.glob(os.path.join(output_dir, "*_转码版.mp4"))
        # 兼容老文件命名
        old_fast_files = glob.glob(os.path.join(output_dir, "*_fast.mp4"))
        fast_files.extend(old_fast_files)
        
        if fast_files:
            return sorted(fast_files, key=os.path.getmtime, reverse=True)[0]
            
        # 最后尝试查找任何mp4文件
        mp4_files = glob.glob(os.path.join(output_dir, "*.mp4"))
        if mp4_files:
            # 排除可能的剪辑输出文件
            non_clip_files = [f for f in mp4_files if "_clip" not in f.lower() and "智能剪辑" not in f.lower()]
            if non_clip_files:
                return sorted(non_clip_files, key=os.path.getmtime, reverse=True)[0]
                
        # 如果都找不到，返回None
        return None
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"查找视频文件时出错: {e}")
        return None

# 尝试加载.env文件中的环境变量
def load_env():
    try:
        from dotenv import load_dotenv
        # 尝试加载.env文件
        env_file = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)), '../../.env')
        if os.path.exists(env_file):
            load_dotenv(env_file)
            print("已加载.env文件中的环境变量配置")
        else:
            print("未找到.env文件，将使用系统环境变量")
    except ImportError:
        print("提示: 安装python-dotenv可以从.env文件加载环境变量")
        print("安装命令: pip install python-dotenv")
        # 如果没有安装dotenv，继续使用系统环境变量 

def fix_subtitle_encoding_and_format(srt_file, output_file=None):
    """
    修复字幕文件的编码问题并规范化格式
    
    Args:
        srt_file: 原始字幕文件路径
        output_file: 输出文件路径，如果为None则覆盖原文件
        
    Returns:
        tuple: (成功标志, 输出文件路径, 使用的编码)
    """
    if output_file is None:
        output_file = srt_file
        
    # 创建输出目录
    output_dir = os.path.dirname(output_file)
    if output_dir and not os.path.exists(output_dir):
        os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)
    
    # 尝试多种编码读取文件
    content = None
    used_encoding = None
    encodings_to_try = ['utf-8-sig', 'utf-8', 'gbk', 'gb2312', 'latin1', 'cp1252']
    
    # 首先尝试常见编码
    for encoding in encodings_to_try:
        try:
            with open(srt_file, 'r', encoding=encoding, errors='ignore') as f:
                content = f.read()
            used_encoding = encoding
            logging.info(f"成功使用 {encoding} 编码读取字幕文件")
            break
        except UnicodeDecodeError:
            continue
    
    # 如果常见编码失败，尝试使用chardet检测
    if content is None:
        try:
            import chardet
            with open(srt_file, 'rb') as f:
                raw_data = f.read()
            result = chardet.detect(raw_data)
            if result['confidence'] > 0.7:
                try:
                    content = raw_data.decode(result['encoding'], errors='ignore')
                    used_encoding = result['encoding']
                    logging.info(f"使用chardet检测到编码: {used_encoding}, 置信度: {result['confidence']}")
                except Exception:
                    pass
        except ImportError:
            logging.warning("chardet库未安装，无法自动检测编码")
    
    # 如果仍然无法读取，尝试二进制方式
    if content is None:
        try:
            with open(srt_file, 'rb') as f:
                content = f.read().decode('utf-8', errors='ignore')
            used_encoding = 'utf-8 (forced)'
            logging.warning(f"使用强制UTF-8解码，可能存在字符丢失")
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"无法读取字幕文件: {str(e)}")
            return False, srt_file, None
    
    # 规范化时间戳格式
    normalized_content = normalize_subtitle_timestamps(content)
    
    # 规范化字幕序号（从0开始）
    normalized_content = normalize_subtitle_numbers(normalized_content)
    
    # 使用UTF-8编码写入输出文件
    try:
        with open(output_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            f.write(normalized_content)
        logging.info(f"成功将字幕文件保存为UTF-8编码: {output_file}")
        return True, output_file, 'utf-8'
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"保存修复后的字幕文件失败: {str(e)}")
        return False, srt_file, used_encoding

def normalize_subtitle_timestamps(content):
    """
    规范化字幕文件中的时间戳格式
    
    Args:
        content: 字幕文件内容
        
    Returns:
        str: 规范化后的内容
    """
    # 匹配SRT时间戳格式
    timestamp_pattern = re.compile(r'(\d{1,2}):(\d{1,2}):(\d{1,2})[,.](\d{1,3})\s*-->\s*(\d{1,2}):(\d{1,2}):(\d{1,2})[,.](\d{1,3})')
    
    def format_timestamp(match):
        h1, m1, s1, ms1, h2, m2, s2, ms2 = match.groups()
        # 确保毫秒是三位数
        ms1 = ms1.ljust(3, '0')[:3]
        ms2 = ms2.ljust(3, '0')[:3]
        return f"{int(h1):02d}:{int(m1):02d}:{int(s1):02d},{ms1} --> {int(h2):02d}:{int(m2):02d}:{int(s2):02d},{ms2}"
    
    # 替换所有时间戳
    return timestamp_pattern.sub(format_timestamp, content)

def normalize_subtitle_numbers(content):
    """
    规范化字幕序号，使其从0开始递增
    
    Args:
        content: 字幕文件内容
        
    Returns:
        str: 规范化后的内容
    """
    lines = content.split('\n')
    normalized_lines = []
    subtitle_index = 0
    in_subtitle_block = False
    
    for i, line in enumerate(lines):
        line = line.strip()
        
        # 检测字幕块的开始（序号行）
        if not in_subtitle_block and line.isdigit():
            normalized_lines.append(str(subtitle_index))
            subtitle_index += 1
            in_subtitle_block = True
        # 检测时间戳行
        elif in_subtitle_block and '-->' in line:
            normalized_lines.append(line)
        # 检测空行（字幕块结束）
        elif line == '':
            normalized_lines.append('')
            in_subtitle_block = False
        # 其他行（字幕内容）
        else:
            normalized_lines.append(line)
    
    return '\n'.join(normalized_lines)

    def _build_task(self, data: Dict[str, Any]) -> UnifiedTask:
        payload = dict(data.get("payload") or {})
        metadata = dict(data.get("metadata") or {})
        source_path = str(
            data.get("source_path")
            or payload.get("source_path")
            or metadata.get("source_path")
            or ""
        ).strip()
        source_url = (
            data.get("url")
            or data.get("source_url")
            or data.get("post_url")
            or metadata.get("post_url")
            or ""
        )

        task_type = parse_task_type(data.get("task_type", metadata.get("task_type", "video")))
        if task_type == TaskType.VIDEO and not source_url and not source_path:
            raise ValueError("missing source url/source path for video task")

        source_url = self._resolve_video_source_url(
            task_type=task_type,
            source_url=str(source_url or "").strip(),
            payload=payload,
            metadata=metadata,
        )

        forum_post_info = self._normalize_forum_post_info(payload=payload, metadata=metadata)
        if forum_post_info:
            metadata["forum_post_info"] = forum_post_info
            payload["forum_post_info"] = forum_post_info

        original_filename = self._resolve_original_filename(
            forum_post_info=forum_post_info,
            payload=payload,
            metadata=metadata,
            source_url=source_url,
        )
        if original_filename:
            metadata["original_filename"] = original_filename
            payload["original_filename"] = original_filename

            max_retries = self.max_retries_default

        try:
            retry_count = max(0, int(retry_count_raw))
        except Exception:
            retry_count = 0

        stage_checkpoint_raw = data.get("stage_checkpoint", metadata.get("stage_checkpoint"))

            current_stage = 0

            stage_checkpoint = str(stage_checkpoint_raw).strip() or None

        metadata.setdefault("source", metadata.get("source", "monitor_dispatch"))

            task_type=task_type,
            source=metadata.get("source", "monitor_dispatch"),

            max_retries=max_retries,
            current_stage=current_stage,
            stage_checkpoint=stage_checkpoint,
        )
        self._sync_task_metadata(task)

        return task

    def _apply_video_output_naming(self, task: UnifiedTask, result: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        normalized_result = dict(result or {})
        output_path = str(normalized_result.get("output_path") or "").strip()
        if not output_path:
            return normalized_result

        metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
        original_filename = self._resolve_original_filename(
            forum_post_info=metadata.get("forum_post_info"),
            payload=task.payload,
            metadata=metadata,
            source_url=str(task.source_url or ""),
        )
        if not original_filename:
            return normalized_result
        if self._is_final_output_already_equivalent(
            output_path=output_path,
            original_filename=original_filename,
        ):
            metadata["original_filename"] = original_filename
            metadata["named_output_path"] = output_path
            task.metadata = metadata
            return normalized_result

        try:
            named_output_path = self._resolve_named_output_path(
                output_path=output_path,
                original_filename=original_filename,
            )
        except Exception as exc:
            self.logger.warning(
                "output naming fallback to stage output: task=%s err=%s",
                task.task_id,
                exc,
            )
            return normalized_result

        metadata["original_filename"] = original_filename
        metadata["named_output_path"] = named_output_path
        task.metadata = metadata

        if named_output_path != output_path:
            normalized_result["original_output_path"] = output_path
            normalized_result["named_output_path"] = named_output_path
            normalized_result["output_path"] = named_output_path
        return normalized_result

    def _is_final_output_already_equivalent(self, output_path: str, original_filename: str) -> bool:
        output_file = Path(str(output_path or "").strip())
        output_name = output_file.name
        if not output_name:
            return False
        parsed = Path(self._sanitize_filename(original_filename))
        stem = parsed.stem if parsed.suffix else parsed.name
        if not stem:
            return False
        suffix = parsed.suffix or output_file.suffix or ".mp4"
        expected = f"{stem}_final{suffix}"
        return output_name.lower() == expected.lower()

    def _resolve_named_output_path(self, output_path: str, original_filename: str) -> str:
        source = Path(str(output_path).strip())
        if not source.exists():
            return str(source)

        sanitized = self._sanitize_filename(original_filename)
        if not sanitized:
            return str(source)
        parsed = Path(sanitized)
        stem = parsed.stem if parsed.suffix else parsed.name
        if not stem:
            return str(source)
        suffix = parsed.suffix or source.suffix or ".mp4"
        candidate = source.with_name(f"{stem}{suffix}")
        if candidate.resolve() == source.resolve():
            return str(source)

        selected = candidate
        index = 1
        while selected.exists():
            selected = source.with_name(f"{stem}_{index}{suffix}")
            index += 1

        shutil.copy2(source, selected)
        return str(selected)

    def _resolve_download_filename(self, task: UnifiedTask, source_url: str) -> str:
        guessed = self._guess_download_filename(source_url)
        original_filename = self._resolve_original_filename(
            forum_post_info=(task.metadata or {}).get("forum_post_info"),
            payload=task.payload,
            metadata=task.metadata,
            source_url=source_url,
        )
        if not original_filename:
            return guessed

        parsed_original = Path(original_filename)
        stem = self._sanitize_filename(parsed_original.stem if parsed_original.suffix else parsed_original.name)
        if not stem:
            return guessed
        suffix = parsed_original.suffix or Path(guessed).suffix or ".mp4"
        return f"{stem}{suffix}"

    def _resolve_video_source_url(
        self,
        task_type: TaskType,
        source_url: str,
        payload: Dict[str, Any],
        metadata: Dict[str, Any],
    ) -> str:
        if task_type != TaskType.VIDEO:
            return source_url

        fallback_video_url = self._pick_first_video_url(payload=payload, metadata=metadata)
        if not source_url:
            return fallback_video_url
        return source_url

    def _pick_first_video_url(self, payload: Dict[str, Any], metadata: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
        candidates: List[str] = []
        for bucket in (
            payload.get("video_urls"),
            metadata.get("video_urls"),
            (payload.get("forum_post_info") or {}).get("video_urls")
            if isinstance(payload.get("forum_post_info"), dict)
            else [],
            (metadata.get("forum_post_info") or {}).get("video_urls")
            if isinstance(metadata.get("forum_post_info"), dict)
            else [],
        ):
            if not isinstance(bucket, list):
                continue
            for item in bucket:
                text = str(item or "").strip()
                if text:
                    candidates.append(text)
        return candidates[0] if candidates else ""

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import asdict, dataclass, field
from datetime import datetime
from enum import Enum
import json
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional


class TaskType(str, Enum):
    VIDEO = "video"
    TTS = "tts"
    VOICE_CLONE = "voice_clone"
    IMAGE = "image"


class TaskStatus(str, Enum):
    PENDING = "pending"
    ASSIGNED = "assigned"
    DOWNLOADING = "downloading"
    PROCESSING = "processing"
    UPLOADING = "uploading"
    COMPLETED = "completed"
    FAILED = "failed"
    CANCELLED = "cancelled"


ALLOWED_STATUS_TRANSITIONS = {
    TaskStatus.PENDING: {
        TaskStatus.ASSIGNED,
        TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING,
        TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
        TaskStatus.FAILED,
        TaskStatus.CANCELLED,
    },
    TaskStatus.ASSIGNED: {
        TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING,
        TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
        TaskStatus.FAILED,
        TaskStatus.CANCELLED,
    },
    TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING: {
        TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
        TaskStatus.FAILED,
        TaskStatus.CANCELLED,
    },
    TaskStatus.PROCESSING: {
        TaskStatus.UPLOADING,
        TaskStatus.COMPLETED,
        TaskStatus.FAILED,
        TaskStatus.CANCELLED,
    },
    TaskStatus.UPLOADING: {
        TaskStatus.COMPLETED,
        TaskStatus.FAILED,
        TaskStatus.CANCELLED,
    },
    TaskStatus.COMPLETED: set(),
    TaskStatus.FAILED: {
        TaskStatus.PENDING,
        TaskStatus.CANCELLED,
    },
    TaskStatus.CANCELLED: set(),
}


class TaskPriority(int, Enum):
    URGENT = 0
    HIGH = 1
    NORMAL = 2
    LOW = 3


def parse_task_type(value: Any) -> TaskType:
    if isinstance(value, TaskType):
        return value
    if isinstance(value, str):
        lowered = value.strip().lower()
        try:
            return TaskType(lowered)
        except ValueError:
            try:
                return TaskType[value.strip().upper()]
            except KeyError:
                return TaskType.VIDEO
    return TaskType.VIDEO


def parse_task_status(value: Any) -> TaskStatus:
    if isinstance(value, TaskStatus):
        return value
    if isinstance(value, str):
        lowered = value.strip().lower()
        try:
            return TaskStatus(lowered)
        except ValueError:
            try:
                return TaskStatus[value.strip().upper()]
            except KeyError:
                return TaskStatus.PENDING
    return TaskStatus.PENDING


def parse_task_priority(value: Any) -> TaskPriority:
    if isinstance(value, TaskPriority):
        return value
    if isinstance(value, int):
        try:
            return TaskPriority(value)
        except ValueError:
            return TaskPriority.NORMAL
    if isinstance(value, str):
        v = value.strip().lower()
        name_map = {
            "urgent": TaskPriority.URGENT,
            "high": TaskPriority.HIGH,
            "normal": TaskPriority.NORMAL,
            "low": TaskPriority.LOW,
        }
        if v in name_map:
            return name_map[v]
        if v.isdigit():
            try:
                return TaskPriority(int(v))
            except ValueError:
                return TaskPriority.NORMAL
    return TaskPriority.NORMAL


def can_transition_status(old_status: Any, new_status: Any) -> bool:
    old = parse_task_status(old_status)
    new = parse_task_status(new_status)
    if old == new:
        return True
    return new in ALLOWED_STATUS_TRANSITIONS.get(old, set())


@dataclass(order=True)
class UnifiedTask:
    sort_key: tuple = field(init=False, repr=False)

    task_id: str
    task_type: TaskType
    source: str

    source_url: Optional[str] = None
    source_path: Optional[str] = None

    status: TaskStatus = TaskStatus.PENDING
    priority: TaskPriority = TaskPriority.NORMAL

    created_at: datetime = field(default_factory=datetime.now)
    assigned_at: Optional[datetime] = None
    started_at: Optional[datetime] = None
    completed_at: Optional[datetime] = None

    payload: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)

    result: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
    error_message: Optional[str] = None

    retry_count: int = 0
    max_retries: int = 3
    current_stage: int = 0
    stage_checkpoint: Optional[str] = None

    worker_id: Optional[str] = None
    worker_url: Optional[str] = None

    output_path: Optional[str] = None
    output_files: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)

    def __post_init__(self) -> None:
        self.task_type = parse_task_type(self.task_type)
        self.status = parse_task_status(self.status)
        self.priority = parse_task_priority(self.priority)
        try:
            self.current_stage = max(0, int(self.current_stage))
        except Exception:
            self.current_stage = 0
        if self.stage_checkpoint is not None:
            self.stage_checkpoint = str(self.stage_checkpoint).strip() or None
        self.sort_key = (int(self.priority), self.created_at)

    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        data = asdict(self)
        # sort_key is an internal ordering field and must not be part of serialized payload.
        data.pop("sort_key", None)
        data["task_type"] = self.task_type.value
        data["status"] = self.status.value
        data["priority"] = int(self.priority)
        data["created_at"] = self.created_at.isoformat()
        data["assigned_at"] = self.assigned_at.isoformat() if self.assigned_at else None
        data["started_at"] = self.started_at.isoformat() if self.started_at else None
        data["completed_at"] = self.completed_at.isoformat() if self.completed_at else None
        return data

    @classmethod
    def from_dict(cls, data: Dict[str, Any]) -> "UnifiedTask":
        copy = dict(data)
        copy.pop("sort_key", None)
        for key in ("created_at", "assigned_at", "started_at", "completed_at"):
            if copy.get(key) and isinstance(copy[key], str):
                copy[key] = datetime.fromisoformat(copy[key])
        return cls(**copy)

    def to_json(self) -> str:
        return json.dumps(self.to_dict(), ensure_ascii=False)

    @classmethod
    def from_json(cls, payload: str) -> "UnifiedTask":
        parsed = json.loads(payload)
        if not isinstance(parsed, dict):
            raise ValueError("invalid task json payload")
        return cls.from_dict(parsed)

还有一个隐藏关键点我在确认中：stage8 现在不是直接吃任务 payload，它主要从 output_dir/forum_post_info.json 取封面信息。所以如果我们要让 worker 真正带着论坛上下文跑内部流水线，除了改 stage5/stage6，还得把这份上下文文件在任务目录里准备好。这样 OpenClaw/worker 传下来的标题、热词才不会在流水线里丢失。

    def _prepare_video_download_context(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> None:
        if task.task_type != TaskType.VIDEO:
            return
        metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
        payload = dict(task.payload or {})
        forum_info: Dict[str, Any] = {}
        if isinstance(metadata.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
            forum_info.update(metadata.get("forum_post_info") or {})
        if isinstance(payload.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
            forum_info.update(payload.get("forum_post_info") or {})

        post_url = self._pick_first_text(
            forum_info.get("post_url"),
            payload.get("post_url"),
            metadata.get("post_url"),
        )
        source_url = str(task.source_url or "").strip()
        if not post_url and self._looks_like_forum_post_url(source_url):
            post_url = source_url
        if post_url:
            forum_info["post_url"] = post_url

        should_parse_post = bool(post_url) and (
            not source_url or self._looks_like_forum_post_url(source_url)
        )
        if should_parse_post:
            parsed_info = self._resolve_forum_post_download_info(post_url)
            forum_info.update(parsed_info)
            parsed_video_url = str(parsed_info.get("video_url") or "").strip()
            if parsed_video_url:
                task.source_url = parsed_video_url

        if forum_info:
            metadata["forum_post_info"] = forum_info
            payload["forum_post_info"] = forum_info

        original_filename = self._resolve_original_filename(
            forum_post_info=forum_info,
            payload=payload,
            metadata=metadata,
            source_url=str(task.source_url or ""),
        )
        if original_filename:
            metadata["original_filename"] = original_filename
            payload["original_filename"] = original_filename
            if forum_info:
                forum_info["original_filename"] = original_filename
                metadata["forum_post_info"] = forum_info
                payload["forum_post_info"] = forum_info

        task.metadata = metadata
        task.payload = payload

    def _resolve_forum_post_download_info(self, post_url: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        normalized_post_url = str(post_url or "").strip()
        if not normalized_post_url:
            return {}
        base_url = self._resolve_forum_base_url(normalized_post_url)
        forum_cfg = self._resolve_forum_upload_config()
        client = ForumHttpClient(
            base_url=base_url,
            username=forum_cfg.get("username", ""),
            password=forum_cfg.get("password", ""),
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        crawler = ForumCrawler(http_client=client, logger=self.logger)
        detail = crawler.fetch_thread_detail(normalized_post_url)
        if detail is None:
            raise RuntimeError(f"failed to parse forum post detail: {normalized_post_url}")

        detail_dict = detail.to_dict()
        processor = ForumContentProcessor(logger=self.logger)
        parsed_info = processor.build_forum_post_info(detail_dict)

        video_urls: List[str] = []
        for item in detail.video_urls:
            text = str(item or "").strip()
            if text:
                video_urls.append(text)
        for item in parsed_info.get("video_urls", []) if isinstance(parsed_info, dict) else []:
            text = str(item or "").strip()
            if text:
                video_urls.append(text)
        dedup_video_urls: List[str] = []
        seen_urls: set[str] = set()
        for item in video_urls:
            if item in seen_urls:
                continue
            seen_urls.add(item)
            dedup_video_urls.append(item)
        if not dedup_video_urls:
            raise RuntimeError(f"no downloadable video url found in post: {normalized_post_url}")
        video_url = dedup_video_urls[0]

        thread_id = self._pick_first_text(
            parsed_info.get("thread_id"),
            detail.thread_id,
            self._parse_thread_id_from_post_url(normalized_post_url),
        )
        post_id = self._pick_first_text(
            parsed_info.get("post_id"),
            detail.post_id,
            thread_id,
        )
        original_filename = self._pick_first_text(
            parsed_info.get("original_filename"),
            detail.original_filename,
            self._guess_download_filename(video_url),
        )
        hotwords = self._normalize_text_list(parsed_info.get("hotwords"))
        result: Dict[str, Any] = {
            "post_url": normalized_post_url,
            "thread_id": thread_id,
            "post_id": post_id,
            "title": self._pick_first_text(parsed_info.get("title"), detail.title),
            "author_name": self._pick_first_text(parsed_info.get("author_name"), detail.author_name),
            "author_id": self._pick_first_text(parsed_info.get("author_id"), detail.author_id),
            "video_url": video_url,
            "video_urls": dedup_video_urls,
            "original_filename": self._sanitize_filename(original_filename),
            "cover_title_up": self._pick_first_text(parsed_info.get("cover_title_up"), detail.cover_title_up),
            "cover_title_middle": self._pick_first_text(
                parsed_info.get("cover_title_middle"),
                detail.cover_title_middle,
            ),
            "cover_title_down": self._pick_first_text(parsed_info.get("cover_title_down"), detail.cover_title_down),
        }
        if hotwords:
            result["hotwords"] = hotwords
        return result

    def _resolve_forum_base_url(self, post_url: str) -> str:
        configured = str(self._resolve_forum_upload_config().get("base_url", "")).strip()
        if configured:
            return configured
        parsed = urlparse(str(post_url or "").strip())
        if parsed.scheme and parsed.netloc:
            return f"{parsed.scheme}://{parsed.netloc}"
        raise RuntimeError(f"unable to resolve forum base url from post_url: {post_url}")

    def _write_forum_post_info_snapshot(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> None:
        metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
        payload = dict(task.payload or {})
        forum_info = metadata.get("forum_post_info")
        if not isinstance(forum_info, dict) or not forum_info:
            return

        original_filename = self._resolve_original_filename(
            forum_post_info=forum_info,
            payload=payload,
            metadata=metadata,
            source_url=str(task.source_url or ""),
        )
        if not original_filename:
            return
        normalized_name = Path(self._sanitize_filename(original_filename))
        folder_name = normalized_name.stem if normalized_name.suffix else normalized_name.name
        folder_name = self._sanitize_filename(folder_name)
        if not folder_name:
            return

        output_dir = Path(self.config.output_dir) / folder_name
        output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        snapshot_path = output_dir / "forum_post_info.json"
        snapshot_payload = dict(forum_info)
        snapshot_payload["original_filename"] = original_filename
        if str(task.source_url or "").strip():
            snapshot_payload.setdefault("video_url", str(task.source_url or "").strip())
        snapshot_path.write_text(
            json.dumps(snapshot_payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2),
            encoding="utf-8",
        )
        metadata["forum_post_info_path"] = str(snapshot_path)
        metadata["forum_post_info"] = snapshot_payload
        payload["forum_post_info"] = snapshot_payload
        task.metadata = metadata
        task.payload = payload

    def _guess_download_filename(self, source_url: str) -> str:
        parsed = urlparse(source_url)
        raw_name = Path(unquote(parsed.path or "")).name
        if not raw_name.strip():
            return "source.mp4"
        if "." not in raw_name:
            return f"{raw_name}.mp4"
        return raw_name

    def _parse_file_uri(self, source_url: str) -> Path:
        parsed = urlparse(source_url)
        path = unquote(parsed.path or "")
        if path.startswith("/") and len(path) >= 3 and path[2] == ":":
            path = path[1:]
        return Path(path)

    def _looks_like_windows_path(self, value: str) -> bool:
        if len(value) < 3:
            return False
        return value[1] == ":" and value[0].isalpha() and value[2] in {"/", "\\"}

    def _upload_output(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        output_path = str(task.output_path or "").strip()
        if not output_path:
            raise ValueError("missing output_path for upload")
        source = Path(output_path)
        if not source.exists():
            raise FileNotFoundError(f"output file not found: {source}")
        local_result = self.storage_adapter.upload(task_id=task.task_id, source_path=str(source))
        upload_result = dict(local_result)
        upload_result["forum_reply"] = self._upload_forum_reply_if_needed(task=task, source=source)
        return upload_result

    def _upload_forum_reply_if_needed(self, task: UnifiedTask, source: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        if task.task_type != TaskType.VIDEO:
            return {"attempted": False, "success": False, "reason": "non_video_task"}
        if not self.forum_upload_enabled:
            return {"attempted": False, "success": False, "reason": "forum_upload_disabled"}

        thread_id, has_forum_target = self._resolve_upload_thread_id(task)
        if not has_forum_target:
            return {"attempted": False, "success": False, "reason": "no_forum_thread"}
        if not thread_id:
            raise NonRetryableUploadError("forum thread_id is missing and cannot be parsed from post_url")

        forum_cfg = self._resolve_forum_upload_config()
        base_url = forum_cfg.get("base_url", "")
        username = forum_cfg.get("username", "")
        password = forum_cfg.get("password", "")
        if not base_url or not username or not password:
            raise NonRetryableUploadError(
                "forum upload config missing: FORUM_BASE_URL/FORUM_USERNAME/FORUM_PASSWORD"
            )

        client = ForumHttpClient(
            base_url=base_url,
            username=username,
            password=password,
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        replier = ForumReplier(http_client=client, logger=self.logger)
        reply_content = self._resolve_forum_reply_content(task=task)
        ok, err = replier.reply_with_attachments(
            thread_id=thread_id,
            content=reply_content,
            video_files=[str(source)],
            strict_attachment=True,
        )
        if not ok:
            message = f"forum reply with attachment failed: {err}"
            if self._is_retryable_forum_error(err):
                raise RetryableUploadError(message)
            raise NonRetryableUploadError(message)
        return {
            "attempted": True,
            "success": True,
            "thread_id": thread_id,
            "strict_attachment": True,
        }

    def _resolve_forum_reply_content(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> str:
        metadata = task.metadata if isinstance(task.metadata, dict) else {}
        payload = task.payload if isinstance(task.payload, dict) else {}
        forum_info: Dict[str, Any] = {}
        if isinstance(payload.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
            forum_info.update(payload.get("forum_post_info") or {})
        if isinstance(metadata.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
            forum_info.update(metadata.get("forum_post_info") or {})

        user_report = self._pick_first_text(
            metadata.get("user_report"),
            payload.get("user_report"),
            forum_info.get("user_report"),
        )
        if user_report:
            return user_report
