+    def _prepare_internal_pipeline_context(self, task: UnifiedTask, task_dir: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+        payload = task.payload if isinstance(task.payload, dict) else {}
+        metadata = task.metadata if isinstance(task.metadata, dict) else {}
+        options: Dict[str, Any] = {}
+
+        forum_info = self._normalize_forum_post_info(payload=payload, metadata=metadata)
+        if isinstance(payload.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
+            forum_info.update(payload.get("forum_post_info") or {})
+        if isinstance(metadata.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
+            forum_info.update(metadata.get("forum_post_info") or {})
+
+        original_filename = self._resolve_original_filename(
+            forum_post_info=forum_info,
+            payload=payload,
+            metadata=metadata,
+            source_url=str(task.source_url or ""),
+        )
+        if original_filename:
+            forum_info["original_filename"] = original_filename
+
+        if forum_info:
+            forum_post_info_path = task_dir / "forum_post_info.json"
+            forum_post_info_path.write_text(
+                json.dumps(forum_info, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2),
+                encoding="utf-8",
+            )
+            options["forum_post_info_json"] = str(forum_post_info_path)
+
+            next_metadata = dict(metadata)
+            next_payload = dict(payload)
+            next_metadata["forum_post_info"] = forum_info
+            next_metadata["internal_pipeline_forum_post_info_path"] = str(forum_post_info_path)
+            next_payload["forum_post_info"] = forum_info
+            task.metadata = next_metadata
+            task.payload = next_payload
+            metadata = next_metadata
+            payload = next_payload
+
+        stage5_model_name = self._pick_first_text(
+            payload.get("stage5_model_name"),
+            metadata.get("stage5_model_name"),
+            payload.get("model_name"),
+            metadata.get("model_name"),
+        )
+        if stage5_model_name:
+            options["model"] = stage5_model_name
+
+        file_encoding = self._pick_first_text(
+            payload.get("stage5_file_encoding"),
+            metadata.get("stage5_file_encoding"),
+            payload.get("file_encoding"),
+            metadata.get("file_encoding"),
+        )
+        if file_encoding:
+            options["file_encoding"] = file_encoding
+
+        stage5_use_preprocessor = self._extract_optional_bool(
+            payload.get("stage5_use_preprocessor"),
+            metadata.get("stage5_use_preprocessor"),
+            payload.get("use_preprocessor"),
+            metadata.get("use_preprocessor"),

+                metadata.get("clip_text_file"),

+    def _append_internal_pipeline_args(self, cmd: List[str], pipeline_inputs: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:
+        model_name = str(pipeline_inputs.get("model") or "").strip()
+        if model_name:
+            cmd.extend(["--model", model_name])
+
+        file_encoding = str(pipeline_inputs.get("file_encoding") or "").strip()
+        if file_encoding:
+            cmd.extend(["--file-encoding", file_encoding])
+
+        if "stage5_use_preprocessor" in pipeline_inputs:
+            if bool(pipeline_inputs["stage5_use_preprocessor"]):
+                cmd.append("--enable-preprocess")
+            else:
+                cmd.append("--disable-preprocess")
+
+        clip_text_file = str(pipeline_inputs.get("clip_text_file") or "").strip()
+        if clip_text_file:
+            cmd.extend(["--clip-text-file", clip_text_file])
+
+        forum_post_info_json = str(pipeline_inputs.get("forum_post_info_json") or "").strip()
+        if forum_post_info_json:
+            cmd.extend(["--forum-post-info-json", forum_post_info_json])
+
+        # Keep root artifacts for worker resolution instead of letting stage9 delete them.
+        cmd.extend(["--organize-delete-original", "false"])

     def _bool_cfg(self, raw: Optional[str], default: bool) -> bool:
         if raw is None:
             return default
         return raw.strip().lower() == "true"
+
+    def _extract_optional_bool(self, *values: Any) -> Optional[bool]:
+        for value in values:
+            if value is None:
+                continue
+            if isinstance(value, bool):
+                return value
+            text = str(value).strip().lower()
+            if not text:
+                continue
+            if text in {"1", "true", "yes", "y", "on"}:
+                return True
+            if text in {"0", "false", "no", "n", "off"}:
+                return False
+        return None

+    def _prepare_internal_pipeline_context(self, task: UnifiedTask, task_dir: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+        payload = task.payload if isinstance(task.payload, dict) else {}
+        metadata = task.metadata if isinstance(task.metadata, dict) else {}
+        options: Dict[str, Any] = {}
+
+        forum_info = self._normalize_forum_post_info(payload=payload, metadata=metadata)
+        if isinstance(payload.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
+            forum_info.update(payload.get("forum_post_info") or {})
+        if isinstance(metadata.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
+            forum_info.update(metadata.get("forum_post_info") or {})
+
+        original_filename = self._resolve_original_filename(
+            forum_post_info=forum_info,
+            payload=payload,
+            metadata=metadata,
+            source_url=str(task.source_url or ""),
+        )
+        if original_filename:
+            forum_info["original_filename"] = original_filename
+
+        if forum_info:
+            forum_post_info_path = task_dir / "forum_post_info.json"
+            forum_post_info_path.write_text(
+                json.dumps(forum_info, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2),
+                encoding="utf-8",
+            )
+            options["forum_post_info_json"] = str(forum_post_info_path)
+
+            next_metadata = dict(metadata)
+            next_payload = dict(payload)
+            next_metadata["forum_post_info"] = forum_info
+            next_metadata["internal_pipeline_forum_post_info_path"] = str(forum_post_info_path)
+            next_payload["forum_post_info"] = forum_info
+            task.metadata = next_metadata
+            task.payload = next_payload
+            metadata = next_metadata
+            payload = next_payload
+
+        stage5_model_name = self._pick_first_text(
+            payload.get("stage5_model_name"),
+            metadata.get("stage5_model_name"),
+            payload.get("model_name"),
+            metadata.get("model_name"),
+        )

+            options["model"] = stage5_model_name
+
+        file_encoding = self._pick_first_text(
+            payload.get("stage5_file_encoding"),
+            metadata.get("stage5_file_encoding"),
+            payload.get("file_encoding"),
+            metadata.get("file_encoding"),
+        )
+        if file_encoding:
+            options["file_encoding"] = file_encoding
+
+        stage5_use_preprocessor = self._extract_optional_bool(
+            payload.get("stage5_use_preprocessor"),
+            metadata.get("stage5_use_preprocessor"),
+            payload.get("use_preprocessor"),
+            metadata.get("use_preprocessor"),
+        )
+        if stage5_use_preprocessor is not None:
+            options["stage5_use_preprocessor"] = stage5_use_preprocessor

+            clip_text_path.write_text(clip_text, encoding="utf-8")
+            options["clip_text_file"] = str(clip_text_path)
+        else:
+            clip_text_file = self._pick_first_text(
+                payload.get("clip_text_file"),
+                metadata.get("clip_text_file"),
+            )
+            if clip_text_file and Path(clip_text_file).exists():
+                options["clip_text_file"] = clip_text_file
+
+        return options

+            else:

+

+        if clip_text_file:
+            cmd.extend(["--clip-text-file", clip_text_file])
+
+        forum_post_info_json = str(pipeline_inputs.get("forum_post_info_json") or "").strip()
+        if forum_post_info_json:
+            cmd.extend(["--forum-post-info-json", forum_post_info_json])
+
+        # Keep root artifacts for worker resolution instead of letting stage9 delete them.
+        cmd.extend(["--organize-delete-original", "false"])

+    def _extract_optional_bool(self, *values: Any) -> Optional[bool]:
+        for value in values:
+            if value is None:
+                continue
+            if isinstance(value, bool):
+                return value

+                return True
+            if text in {"0", "false", "no", "n", "off"}:

+def _copy_forum_post_info(forum_post_info_json, output_dir, logger):
+    if not forum_post_info_json:
+        return None
+
+    source = os.path.abspath(forum_post_info_json)
+    if not os.path.exists(source):
+        raise FileNotFoundError(f"forum_post_info.json not found: {source}")
+
+    with open(source, "r", encoding="utf-8") as fh:
+        payload = json.load(fh)
+
+    target = os.path.join(output_dir, "forum_post_info.json")
+    with open(target, "w", encoding="utf-8") as fh:
+        json.dump(payload, fh, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
+
+    logger.info(f"论坛上下文已写入: {target}")
+    return target
+

+
+def _parse_optional_bool(value) -> Optional[bool]:
+    if value is None:
+        return None
+    if isinstance(value, bool):
+        return value
+    text = str(value).strip().lower()
+    if not text:
+        return None
+    if text in {"1", "true", "yes", "y", "on"}:
+        return True
+    if text in {"0", "false", "no", "n", "off"}:
+        return False
+    return None
+
+
+def _is_non_interactive(config) -> bool:
+    if config.get("non_interactive"):
+        return True
+    try:
+        return int(config.get("input_wait_time", 5)) == 0
+    except Exception:
+        return False
+
+
+def _read_text_payload(file_path: str) -> Tuple[Optional[str], Optional[str]]:
+    try:
+        with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
+            content = f.read().strip()
+        if not content:
+            return None, "文件内容为空，请重新输入"
+        return content, None
+    except Exception as e:
+        return None, f"读取文件失败: {e}"
+
+
+def _resolve_stage6_text_input(config, clip_text_file: str) -> Tuple[Optional[str], Optional[str], Optional[str]]:
+    explicit_text = config.get("stage6_clip_text")
+    if explicit_text is not None:
+        text = str(explicit_text).strip()
+        if not text:
+            return None, None, "stage6_clip_text 为空，无法继续执行剪辑"
+        return text, "显式指定的 stage6_clip_text", None
+
+    explicit_file = str(config.get("stage6_clip_text_file") or "").strip()
+    if explicit_file:
+        text, error = _read_text_payload(explicit_file)
+        if error:
+            return None, None, error
+        return text, explicit_file, None
+
+    if _is_non_interactive(config):
+        if not os.path.exists(clip_text_file):
+            return None, None, f"未找到剪辑文本文件: {clip_text_file}"
+        text, error = _read_text_payload(clip_text_file)
+        if error:
+            return None, None, f"读取clip_text.txt失败: {error}"
+        return text, clip_text_file, None
+
+    return None, None, None
+
